	focus = {
		id = SAU_unif_gcc_council
		icon = gcc

		x = 53
		y = 0

			y = 5

				OR = {
					tag = JOR

		}

				}
			}
		}

		cost = 5

		allow_branch = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = JOR
				original_tag = IRQ
				original_tag = YEM
				original_tag = MOR

				original_tag = SAU
				original_tag = QAT
				original_tag = UAE
				original_tag = BHR
				original_tag = KUW
				original_tag = OMA
			}
		}

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

			has_idea = idea_gcc_member_state

			gcc_unity_greater_0 = yes
		}

		bypass = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = gcc_focus_completed_tt
				has_global_flag = SAU_unif_gcc_council_completed
			}

		}

		completion_reward = {
			add_political_power = 75
			set_global_flag = SAU_unif_gcc_council_completed

			base = 10

			set_country_flag = SAU_republic_of_arabia_declared
			remove_ideas = {
				SAU_royal_ulema_alliance_neutral
				birthplace_of_wahhabism

			}
		}

			factor = 1
		}

	#- ===== REPUBLIC OF ARABIA =====
	# Republican alternative tree. Hidden until SAU_declare_republic_of_Arabia_1 sets
	# SAU_republic_of_arabia_declared, which also hides the kings tree (SAU_royal_hub).
	focus = {
		id = SAU_republic_provisional_government
		icon = constitution

		x = 130
		y = 0

		cost = 10

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		available = {
			has_country_flag = SAU_republic_of_arabia_declared
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SAU_republic_provisional_government"
			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.90 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.90 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.90 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				set_partyall_allowed = yes
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^11 = 0 } #Kingdom (House of Saud)
				set_variable = { party_pop_array^12 = 0 } #Caliphate (Al-Qaeda)
				set_country_flag = party11_banned
				set_country_flag = party12_banned
				recalculate_party = yes
			}
			if = { limit = { has_idea = wahabi_ulema } remove_ideas = wahabi_ulema }
			if = { limit = { has_idea = saudi_royal_family } remove_ideas = saudi_royal_family }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

			set_country_flag = SAU_parties_legalized
			add_political_power = 75
			hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.10 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.20 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 19 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 9 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 8 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.10 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 12 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.10 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 21 }
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SAU_republic_first_election_tt
			if = { limit = { has_government = democratic } set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_government = communism } set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = yes } }
			else = { set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = yes } }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.0 days = 1 } }
			add_ideas = the_military
			add_ideas = international_bankers
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
